< text>
I hate shopping, but I love shopping at Tuesday Morning! I always want to go there, and when we do there's always so many things we want to buy.

They carry home furnishings for a good price. We bought curtains, curtain rods, a decorative sign, a giant decorative plate, fake candles, fleece/plush throws, a rug, etc.

Check the back of the store for the discount items. The pastel color stickers indicate various discounts. If there's something you like that you need multiple of (like curtains) buy them while you're there because what they carry is always changing, and when they're out, they're out.<//text>
